class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element  sec-large-font font-black\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<h2><span class=\"font-pink\">When Your Message Moves People,</span> You’ll Never Have to Sell Again.</h2>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element \">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<p>Sick of chasing down clients? Tired of always hustling to make things happen and not having the cash flow and freedom you want? Maybe marketing drains you like it’s a blood-sucking vampire, or worse — you wonder if you’re destined to be a slave to “the grind” forever…</p>\n<p>I’m New York Times best-selling author SUZANNE EVANS. People love to talk about my journey from a struggling secretary making $35,000 a year to seven-figure business owner…</p>\n<p>But what they always leave out is what I did to actually make it happen. Today I’m going to show you how I went from zero to making my first million dollars. Hint: It didn’t involve fancy funnels, internet marketing, or pricey ads.</p>\n<p>But before I let you in on how I did it, I want to ask you…</p>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element  sec-large-font font-black\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<h2>Ever Wonder, “<span class=\"font-pink\">Is This Whole Industry Just One Big Freakin’ Scam?</span>”</h2>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element \">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<p>If so, I get it. Maybe you’ve poured in hundreds of hours and thousands of dollars into seminars, trainings, online courses, books, blogs, online marketing … and you’re still not seeing clients, cash flow, or the success all the gurus talk about. Maybe you even feel ripped off.</p>\n<p>You wonder, <strong><em>“What the hell am I missing?”</em></strong></p>\n<p>Thing is, you know you’re smart, creative, and talented … and you’ve invested in your own growth and personal development. Hell, you might even be certified in your field and hold a ton of degrees. Then you read some success story online or see some person speak at a conference and you just want to throw your damn hands in the air and shout…</p>\n<p><strong><em>“How is THAT person making money, landing gigs, and living the dream when I know I’m just as good or even better?!? What the hell am I missing? Better marketing? A bigger email list? A slick website, professional photos, and a $50,000 Facebook ad budget? What the hell do I need?”</em></strong></p>\n<p>Of course you’d be jaded, skeptical, and leery because here’s the thing:</p>\n<p>No one out there wants to tell you the truth about what it takes to really succeed … but I’m going to.</p>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n<div class=\"vc_btn3-container  blue-button register-btn vc_btn3-center\">\n\t<a class=\"vc_general vc_btn3 vc_btn3-size-lg vc_btn3-shape-rounded vc_btn3-style-flat vc_btn3-color-grey pum-trigger\" href=\"#go-to-register\" title=\"\" style=\"cursor: pointer;\">Register now</a></div>\n</div></div></div><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-2\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\"></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"vc_row-full-width vc_clearfix\"></div><div id=\"section3\" data-vc-full-width=\"true\" data-vc-full-width-init=\"true\" class=\"vc_row wpb_row vc_row-fluid small-padded vc_custom_1484591230427 vc_row-has-fill\" style=\"position: relative; left: -24.25px; box-sizing: border-box; width: 785px; padding-left: 24.25px; padding-right: 23.75px;\"><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-12\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\"><div class=\"vc_row wpb_row vc_inner vc_row-fluid\"><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-2\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\"></div></div></div><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-8\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element  testimonial-box\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<div class=\"testimonial-box-wrapper white-bg\">\n<p><strong>“</strong>Speaking has been and continues to be a key strategic part of my growth trajectory and catapulting my agency’s brand. In one speaking event in front of 5,000 attendees, I was able to generate 800 new leads, $350k in sales, and partnership opportunities with other leading businesses.<strong>”</strong></p>\n</div>\n<p><img src=\"/wp-content/uploads/2017/01/re-testimonial.png\" alt=\"\"><br>\n<span class=\"author-name\">Re Perez</span><br>\n<span class=\"author-desc white\">Branding For The People</span></p>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element  vc_custom_1484619525819 sec-header-font font-white\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<h2>The #1 Reason Most People Fail is Because They’re Trying to Market A Business … Instead Of Starting A Movement!</h2>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n</div></div></div><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-2\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\"></div></div></div></div><div class=\"vc_row wpb_row vc_inner vc_row-fluid\"><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-2\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\"></div></div></div><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-8\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element  font-white\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<p>The secret to my success – and yours – is that you’ve got to focus on creating a MOVEMENT. Don’t get me wrong: marketing is important to business. Marketers teach tactics, strategies, systems, and technology… but no marketer can teach you to create your MOVEMENT because a movement has to come from you. It has to come from your WHY.</p>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element  font-white font-marvel\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<h2>Marketing a business that doesn’t have a MOVEMENT behind it is like putting lipstick on a pig.</h2>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element  font-white\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<p>That would be crazy, but people do this all the time in business. That’s why they fail: there’s no substance, no pull of the heartstrings, no emotion, no transformation, no WHY … no wonder there are no clients, cash flow or followers! When a business puts making a buck ahead of making a difference, it’s dead before it even begins. So take it from me…</p>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n</div></div></div><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-2\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\"></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"vc_row-full-width vc_clearfix\"></div><div id=\"section4\" data-vc-full-width=\"true\" data-vc-full-width-init=\"true\" class=\"vc_row wpb_row vc_row-fluid small-padded vc_custom_1484627197928 vc_row-has-fill\" style=\"position: relative; left: -24.25px; box-sizing: border-box; width: 785px; padding-left: 24.25px; padding-right: 23.75px;\"><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-12\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\"><div class=\"vc_row wpb_row vc_inner vc_row-fluid\"><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-2\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\"></div></div></div><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-8\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element  sec-large-font font-white\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<h2 class=\"font-pink\">Building A Great Business Isn’t About Moving Products or Marketing.<span class=\"font-white\">It’s About Moving People.</span></h2>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element  font-white\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<p>Think about the brands we know, like, trust, and even love. Apple. TOMS shoes. Starbucks. Uber. Star Wars. These aren’t brands powered by some swanky agency on Madison Avenue. These are MOVEMENTS. People follow, flock, and fight for these names.</p>\n<p>(Hell, you should see how pissed I get when I’m in a city that DOESN’T have Uber … and I lived in NYC for years taking yellow cabs everywhere! Uber isn’t just a business, it’s a movement.)</p>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element  sec-large-font font-white font-center\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<h2>You Might Be Thinking: “Easy For YOU, Suzanne. But…”</h2>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element  font-white\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<p>Look, I didn’t go from zero to my first million dollars because I was a great marketer. Please! I was a secretary making $35,000 a year and my father was a farmer … I wasn’t exactly the second coming of Peggy Olsen from Mad Men. When I started in 2005, I was bored, broke, and $100,000 in debt.</p>\n<p>I started my business somewhere between the organic tomatoes and bananas at my local Whole Foods. I draped a simple folding table with some poorly cut fabric from Wal-Mart. (Far from Instagram-worthy!) All I had in my hand: 100 poorly printed business cards that would make any designer cringe. My logo? Printed in blurry ink on crappy cardstock from Staples. Here’s some marketing for you … I had:</p>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n\n\t<div class=\"wpb_raw_code wpb_content_element wpb_raw_html\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<div class=\"pinkxlist\">\n<ul class=\"sec4list\">\n<li>no website</li>\n<li>no email list</li>\n<li>no Facebook “fans”</li>\n<li>no YouTube subscribers</li>\n</ul>\n<ul class=\"sec4list\">\n<li>no Instagram followers</li>\n<li>no fancy funnels, five-step formulas, or Facebook ads</li>\n<li>...Hell, I didn’t even have a damn brochure!</li>\n</ul>\n\n<div class=\"sp-clear\"></div>\n</div>\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element  testimonial-box\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<div class=\"testimonial-box-wrapper\">\n<p><strong>“</strong>In January of 2016, I took a stage with 8 people in the room and closed half of them for a total of $16,000. I went on to create another $59,000 from what I learned about speaking from Suzanne.</p>\n<p>I’ve sold a retail business I had, and am headed for $200,000 from speaking in 2017.<strong>”</strong></p>\n</div>\n<p><img src=\"/wp-content/uploads/2017/01/jean-kuhn.png\" alt=\"\"><br>\n<span class=\"author-name\">Jean Kuhn</span><br>\n<span class=\"author-desc white\">www.JeanKuhn.com</span></p>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element  font-white\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<p>Thank God I didn’t meet any internet marketers back then. They would have sent me down any one of eighteen different rabbit holes to “optimize my reach” or “increase my conversion rate” or “generate inbound leads” … meanwhile, I’d be just as broke, freezing my ass off in the produce section of Whole Foods, with zero paying clients.</p>\n<p>But … one thing I had that no one could ever take away from me was a message that moved people. That’s how I built my business. Years later (and I’m gonna tell it like is):</p>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n<div class=\"vc_btn3-container  blue-button register-btn vc_btn3-center\">\n\t<a class=\"vc_general vc_btn3 vc_btn3-size-lg vc_btn3-shape-rounded vc_btn3-style-flat vc_btn3-color-grey pum-trigger\" href=\"#go-to-register\" title=\"\" style=\"cursor: pointer;\">Register now</a></div>\n</div></div></div><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-2\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\"></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"vc_row-full-width vc_clearfix\"></div><div id=\"section5\" data-vc-full-width=\"true\" data-vc-full-width-init=\"true\" class=\"vc_row wpb_row vc_row-fluid not-padded vc_custom_1484374850626 vc_row-has-fill\" style=\"position: relative; left: -24.25px; box-sizing: border-box; width: 785px; padding-left: 24.25px; padding-right: 23.75px;\"><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-12\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\"><div class=\"vc_row wpb_row vc_inner vc_row-fluid vc_custom_1483729614757 vc_row-has-fill\"><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-3\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\"></div></div></div><div class=\"clear-white-bg wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-9\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner vc_custom_1484524422151\"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element  sec-large-font font-black\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<h2 style=\"font-size: 36px;\">…It Feels Pretty Damn Great To Go From A Struggling Secretary Making $35K A Year To $35 MILLION (!!!) Over The Past Seven Years … <span class=\"font-pink\">Speaking To Packed Out Crowds, Working With The Best Talent, and Making A Difference In The Lives Of My Clients and Loved Ones.</span></h2>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element  font-black\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<p>I won’t apologize for saying that … because I want the same for you! Can you imagine how good that would feel? To have clients chase you down instead of the other way around? To know you can spend everyday of your life doing work you actually love and believe in? To make more money than you ever have before, so you can live the life and afford the things and experiences you’ve always dreamed of?</p>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element  marvel-font font-black\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<h2>It’s possible, because when your message moves people, you’ll never have to sell again.</h2>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element  font-black\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<p>That means that whenever you SPEAK, you have the potential to land clients. It means that wherever and whenever you SPEAK out about your movement, the right people will flock to, follow, and finance your business.</p>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n</div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"vc_row-full-width vc_clearfix\"></div><div id=\"section6\" data-vc-full-width=\"true\" data-vc-full-width-init=\"true\" class=\"vc_row wpb_row vc_row-fluid not-padded vc_custom_1484524152978 vc_row-has-fill\" style=\"position: relative; left: -24.25px; box-sizing: border-box; width: 785px; padding-left: 24.25px; padding-right: 23.75px;\"><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-12\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\"><div class=\"vc_row wpb_row vc_inner vc_row-fluid vc_custom_1483729614757 vc_row-has-fill\"><div class=\"clear-pink-bg wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-8\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner vc_custom_1484524280969\"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element  sec-large-font font-white\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<h2>Calling All Change-Makers, Trendsetters, Thought Leaders, Business Owners … It’s Time to Start Your Movement.</h2>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element  font-white\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<p>Starting a movement is all about finding your WHY. Why did Apple become such a rabid movement? Because Steve Jobs was clear on his WHY, to create elegant, sleek devices that changed the way we interact with the world. Why is TOMS Shoes such a beloved brand? Because Blake Mycoskie had a WHY: to provide for someone in need with every purchase.</p>\n<p>We’re not even talking about social, cultural, or religious movements yet … but think about it. Would you call Dr. Martin Luther King Jr. a marketer? Or Mandela? Or Jesus? Or Gandhi? Do you think these people even cared about marketing? Of course not! People followed them because they had a message, belief, and a WHY that was worth following. These people were change-makers, trendsetters, and thought leaders … not marketers. They didn’t chase the paper, they chased a dream … and people followed.</p>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element  testimonial-box\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<div class=\"testimonial-box-wrapper white-bg\">\n<p><strong>“</strong>I walked in to the room and there were only three people, but the show must go on.</p>\n<p>I closed $25,000. Thanks Suzanne!<strong>”</strong></p>\n</div>\n<p><img src=\"/wp-content/uploads/2017/01/carrie-greene.png\" alt=\"\"></p>\n<p><span class=\"author-name\">Carrie Greene </span><br>\n<span class=\"author-desc white\">Carrie Green Coaching</span></p>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n<div class=\"vc_btn3-container  blue-button register-btn vc_btn3-center\">\n\t<a class=\"vc_general vc_btn3 vc_btn3-size-lg vc_btn3-shape-rounded vc_btn3-style-flat vc_btn3-color-grey pum-trigger\" href=\"#go-to-register\" title=\"\" style=\"cursor: pointer;\">Register now</a></div>\n</div></div></div><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-4\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner vc_custom_1484524055605\"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\"></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"vc_row-full-width vc_clearfix\"></div><div id=\"section7\" data-vc-full-width=\"true\" data-vc-full-width-init=\"true\" class=\"vc_row wpb_row vc_row-fluid not-padded vc_custom_1484612164605 vc_row-has-fill\" style=\"position: relative; left: -24.25px; box-sizing: border-box; width: 785px; padding-left: 24.25px; padding-right: 23.75px;\"><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-12\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\"><div class=\"vc_row wpb_row vc_inner vc_row-fluid vc_custom_1483729614757 vc_row-has-fill\"><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-2\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner vc_custom_1484375244287\"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\"></div></div></div><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-8\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner vc_custom_1484629975223\"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element  sec-large-font font-white\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<h2>News Flash: <span class=\"font-pink\">You Are A Living Movement!</span></h2>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element  font-white\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<p>There are millions of people who have a problem you have a solution for. If you have a product or service that makes the world a better place, then it is your responsibility to get your business in front of as many people as possible.</p>\n<p>That’s why you have to start with finding your WHY. Then, when you infuse your marketing with your WHY … you become unstoppable. The two go hand in hand. When your marketing flows out of your movement … and you align profit with passion … your followers will reward you again and again.</p>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element  sec-large-font font-white\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<h2>Remember, Business Still Happens <span class=\"font-pink\">“Eyeball To Eyeball”…</span></h2>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element  font-white\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<p>So, how do you get people to find out about your movement? Easy. You tell them! You get in front of people … one person, ten, or ten thousand … and you SPEAK.</p>\n<p>I’m not talking about becoming a professional speaker. I’m talking about using speaking strategically (in whatever context you’re in) to get word out about your movement. At a coffee shop. In a small group. In a boardroom. Rocking the stage in front of thousands.</p>\n<p>Think back to those names I mentioned earlier. Steve Jobs. Dr. King. Gandhi. Suzanne Evans behind that little table at Whole Foods! None of them were “professional speakers” by trade.</p>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n</div></div></div><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-2\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\"></div></div></div></div><div class=\"vc_row wpb_row vc_inner vc_row-fluid\"><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-2\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\"></div></div></div><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-8\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t<div class=\"wpb_single_image wpb_content_element vc_align_center  vc_custom_1484630077424\">\n\t\t\n\t\t<figure class=\"wpb_wrapper vc_figure\">\n\t\t\t<div class=\"vc_single_image-wrapper   vc_box_border_grey\"><img width=\"957\" height=\"136\" src=\"http://speaksolution.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/01/speech-bubbles-banner.png\" class=\"vc_single_image-img attachment-full\" alt=\"\" srcset=\"http://speaksolution.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/01/speech-bubbles-banner.png 957w, http://speaksolution.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/01/speech-bubbles-banner-300x43.png 300w, http://speaksolution.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/01/speech-bubbles-banner-768x109.png 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 957px) 100vw, 957px\"></div>\n\t\t</figure>\n\t</div>\n</div></div></div><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-2\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\"></div></div></div></div><div class=\"vc_row wpb_row vc_inner vc_row-fluid\"><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-2\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\"></div></div></div><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-8\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element \">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<p class=\"font-white\">But what’s the one thing they did to get word out about their movement? SPEAKING.</p>\n<p class=\"font-white\">So, do you need to land a client? You’ll need to speak to them. Want to promote a product or service? You’ll have to speak about it. Want to make a splash in your market? Apple, to this day, announces new products with someone speaking from a stage. In business and life, speaking is everywhere.</p>\n<p class=\"font-white\">And if you don’t learn how to effectively speak to grow your business, you are stealing from those who need you most.</p>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element  sec-large-font font-white\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<h2>Speaking is the Greatest Tool to Power You To $100,000 A Year (or More) … <span class=\"font-pink\">And It Doesn’t Cost Anything!</span></h2>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element  font-white\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<p>Maybe you’re a coach looking for more clients, or an attorney looking for more cases for your firm. Perhaps you’re a consultant looking for higher-paying gigs, or a speaker looking for bigger stages.</p>\n<p>It doesn’t matter what kind of business you’re in …actually, one of my biggest client success stories was a plumber that went on to become one of the most respected thought leaders in his industry. There was gold in a blue collar industry for this guy! So, I’ve got to ask…</p>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element  testimonial-box\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<div class=\"testimonial-box-wrapper\">\n<p><strong>“</strong>I used to give away my services in the hopes of getting clients. Since training with Suzanne, I recently gave someone else a testimonial and got two new clients. Today, I gave a “save the date announcement” and was asked to speak at a huge local event in March. Even giving my “elevator pitch” now results in getting new paying clients. Learning to “turn my mess into my message” has changed my business from being a secret, to being a success in only seven months.<strong>”</strong></p>\n</div>\n<p><img src=\"/wp-content/uploads/2017/01/jackie-simmons.png\" alt=\"\"></p>\n<p><span class=\"author-name\">Jackie Simmons</span><br>\n<span class=\"author-desc white\">www.TameYourElephants.com</span></p>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n<div class=\"vc_btn3-container  blue-button register-btn vc_btn3-center\">\n\t<a class=\"vc_general vc_btn3 vc_btn3-size-lg vc_btn3-shape-rounded vc_btn3-style-flat vc_btn3-color-grey pum-trigger\" href=\"#go-to-register\" title=\"\" style=\"cursor: pointer;\">Register now</a></div>\n</div></div></div><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-2\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\"></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"vc_row-full-width vc_clearfix\"></div><div id=\"section9\" data-vc-full-width=\"true\" data-vc-full-width-init=\"true\" class=\"vc_row wpb_row vc_row-fluid small-padded\" style=\"position: relative; left: -24.25px; box-sizing: border-box; width: 785px; padding-left: 24.25px; padding-right: 23.75px;\"><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-12\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\"><div class=\"vc_row wpb_row vc_inner vc_row-fluid\"><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-2\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\"></div></div></div><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-8\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element  sec-large-font font-white\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<h2>“What the hell do I really need to work on to earn $100,000 a year (or more) … <span class=\"font-pink\">with the least friction possible?”</span></h2>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element  font-white\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<p>The answer is simple. You don’t need a huge marketing budget, or fancy tech, or a degree from MIT. It starts with SPEAKING to the right people about your movement.</p>\n<p>That’s not to say it will be quick or easy … but like I mentioned earlier, I’m a former secretary and a farmer’s daughter… years later I’m running a multi-million dollar company that’s been featured on the Inc. 500 / 5000 list of fastest growing companies five years in a row.</p>\n<p>It all started with a movement. If I can do it, you can too … and if you let me, I’m going to show you how, step-by-step.</p>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element  testimonial-box\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<div class=\"testimonial-box-wrapper\">\n<p><strong>“</strong>Using Suzanne’s speaking formula I was able to book 56 speeches last year and increase my conversion rate by 20%.<strong>”</strong></p>\n</div>\n<p><img src=\"/wp-content/uploads/2017/01/andy-miller.png\" alt=\"andy miller\"></p>\n<p><span class=\"author-name white-txt\">Andy Miller</span><br>\n<span class=\"author-desc white\">Co-Founder – Big Swift Kick</span></p>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n</div></div></div><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-2\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\"></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"vc_row-full-width vc_clearfix\"></div><div id=\"section11\" data-vc-full-width=\"true\" data-vc-full-width-init=\"true\" class=\"vc_row wpb_row vc_row-fluid small-padded\" style=\"position: relative;
